'mean'),\n).reset_index()\n\n# OOS rate\nstore_oos = inventory.groupby('store_id')['out_of_stock'].mean().reset_index()\nstore_oos.columns = ['store_id', 'oos_rate']\nstore_oos = store_oos.merge(store_primary_rep, on='store_id')\nrep_oos = store_oos.groupby('primary_rep_id')['oos_rate'].mean().reset_index()\nrep_oos.columns = ['rep_id', 'avg_oos_rate']\n\nrep_all = store\nstore_sales = sales.groupby('store_id').agg(\n    total_revenue=('revenue', 'sum'),\n    total_units=('units_sold', 'sum'),\n).reset_index()\n\nstore_data = stores.merge(store_avg_traffic, how='left')\nstore_data['rev_per_sqm'] = store_data['total_revenue'] / store_data['store_size_sqm']\n\n# Z-score within store_type to normalize\nstore_data['rev_per_sqm_z'] = store_data.groupby('store_type')['rev_per_sqm'].transform(\n    lambda x: (x - x.mean()) / x.std()\n)\n\nrep_sales_perf = store_data.groupby('primary_rep_id').agg(\n    avg_rev_per_sqm_z=('rev_per_sqm_z', 'mean'),\n    total_revenue=('total_revenue', 'sum'),\n).reset_index().rename(columns={'primary_rep_id':'rep_id'})\n\n# Visit quality\nvisit_metrics = visits.groupby('rep_id').agg(\n    total_visits=('visit_id', 'count'),\n    completed_visits=('completed_visit', 'sum'),\n    avg_duration=('duration_minutes', 'mean'),\n).reset_index()\nvisit_metrics['completion_rate'] = visit_metrics['completed_visits'] / visit_metrics['total_visits']\n\n# Shelf audit\naudit_with_rep = shelf_audits.merge(visits[['visit_id','rep_id']], on='visit_id')\nshelf_metrics = audit_with_rep.groupby('rep_id').agg(\n    planogram_compliance=('planogram_compliance', 'mean'),\n    avg_facings=('facings', 'mean'),\n    endcap_rate=('endcap_display', 'mean'),\n    checkout_rate=('checkout_display', 'mean'),\n    promo_stand_rate=('promo_stand', 'mean'),\n    pos_materials_rate=('pos_materials', 'mean'),\n).reset_index()\n\n# OOS rate\nstore_oos = inventory.groupby('store_id')['out_of_stock'].mean().reset_index()\nstore_oos.columns = ['store_id', 'oos_rate']\nstore_oos = store_oos.merge(store_primary_rep, on='store_id')\nrep_oos = store_oos.groupby('primary_rep_id')['oos_rate'].mean().reset_index()\nrep_oos.columns = ['rep_id', rep_all.merge(reps[['rep_id','first_name','last_name']], on='rep_id')\n\n# Create z-scores for each metric\ndef zscore(series):\n    return (series - series.mean()) / series.std()\n\n# Activity metrics (higher = better)\nrep_all['z_completion'] = zscore(rep_all['completion_rate'])\nrep_all['z_duration'] = zscore(rep_all['avg_duration'])\nrep_all['z_visits'] = zscore(rep_all['total_visits'])\n# Audit quality (higher = better)\nrep_all['z_planogram'] = zscore(rep_all['planogram_compliance'])\nrep_all['z_facings'] = zscore(rep_all['avg_facings'])\nrep_all['z_endcap'] = zscore(rep_all['endcap_rate'])\nrep_all['z_checkout'] = zscore(rep_all['checkout_rate'])\nrep_all['z_promo'] = zscore(rep_all['promo_stand_rate'])\nrep_all['z_pos'] = zscore(rep_all['pos_materials_rate'])\n# OOS (lower = better, so negate)\nrep_all['z_oos'] = -zscore(rep_all['avg_oos_rate'])\n# Sales outcome\nrep_all['z_sales'] = zscore(rep_all['avg_rev_per_sqm_z'])\n\n# Composite scores\nactivity_z_cols = ['z_completion', 'z_duration', 'z_visits']\naudit_z_cols = ['z_planogram', 'z_facings', rep_all[audit_z_cols].mean(axis=1)\nrep_all['score_outcome'] = rep_all[outcome_z_cols].mean(axis=1)\n\n# Combined: weight activity + audit most (these are directly the rep's wa, wau, wo)\n    z = zscore(score)\n    # Bottom reps at -1.5 std\n    underperforming = rep_all.loc[z < -1.5, 'rep_id'].sort_values().tolist()\n    results[name] = set(underperforming)\n rep_all[['z_oos','z_sales']].mean(axis=1)\n\n# Count how many individual metrics are < -1 std\nindividual_metrics = ['z_completion','z_duration','z_visits','z_planogram','z_facings',\n
